						<div class="elementor-container elementor-column-gap-default">
					<div class="elementor-column elementor-col-50 elementor-top-column elementor-element elementor-element-876fef1" data-id="876fef1" data-element_type="column">
			<div class="elementor-widget-wrap elementor-element-populated">
						<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-43bfb1a elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="43bfb1a" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
					<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">AMAZING SIGIRIYA SRI LANKA</h2>				</div>
				</div>
					</div>
		</div>
				<div class="elementor-column elementor-col-50 elementor-top-column elementor-element elementor-element-af0e70d" data-id="af0e70d" data-element_type="column">
			<div class="elementor-widget-wrap elementor-element-populated">
						<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-a7e2689 elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="a7e2689" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
									<p>Sigiriya Lion Rock is an ancient rock fortress known for its massive column of rock that reaches nearly 200 meters high. The site dates back to the reign of King Kasyapa (477-495 AD), who chose this site as his new capital. He decorated the walls with frescoes, and built an impressive palace right on top of the rock column, accessible only through the mouth of an enormous carved lion.</p>								</div>
				</div>
					</div>
		</div>
					</div>
		</section>

				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
					<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">SIGIRIYA WORLD HERITAGE</h2>				</div>
				</div>
				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-4798dcf elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="4798dcf" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
									<p>The ruins of the capital built by the parricidal King Kassapa (477–95) lie on the steep slopes and at the summit of a granite peak standing some 180m high (the ‘Lion’s Rock’, which dominates the jungle from all sides). A series of galleries and staircases emerging from the mouth of a gigantic lion constructed of bricks and plaster provide access to the site</p>								</div>

				<section class="elementor-section elementor-top-section elementor-element elementor-element-c613218 elementor-section-boxed elementor-section-height-default elementor-section-height-default" data-id="c613218" data-element_type="section" data-settings="{&quot;background_background&quot;:&quot;classic&quot;}">
							<div class="elementor-background-overlay"></div>
							<div class="elementor-container elementor-column-gap-default">
					<div class="elementor-column elementor-col-100 elementor-top-column elementor-element elementor-element-4105088" data-id="4105088" data-element_type="column">
			<div class="elementor-widget-wrap elementor-element-populated">
						<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-8adc458 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="8adc458" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
					<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Sigiriya LION Rock Sri lanka</h2>				</div>
				</div>
				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-2d33f92 elementor-widget-divider--view-line elementor-widget elementor-widget-divider" data-id="2d33f92" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="divider.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
							<div class="elementor-divider">
			<span class="elementor-divider-separator">
						</span>
		</div>
						</div>
				</div>
				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-66884dc elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="66884dc" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
									<p>Sigiriya is one of Sri Lanka&#8217;s most famous historical monuments. Residents call this ancient palace and fortress complex the eighth wonder of the world and it has significant archeology and attracts thousands of tourists annually. This is probably the most visited tourist destination in Sri Lanka.</p><p>The Sigiriya rocky plain, made of magma from an extinct volcano, is 200 meters higher than the surrounding forest. The exhibition surprises visitors with its unique harmony in nature and human imagination.</p><p>Thanks to this lion, the palace got Sigiriya. The word Sigiriya is derived from the word Sihagri, meaning Lion Rock. The western walls of Sigiriya are almost exclusively covered with frescoes, made during the Kasyapa period. Eighteen frescoes are still alive today.</p><p>The fresco depicts a naked woman and is seen as a picture of Kasyapa&#8217;s wife and concubine, or as a priest containing religious rites. Although the identity of the unknown woman is depicted in the mural, this unique ancient painting celebrates the beauty of women and has a remarkable historical impact.</p><p>One of the best features of Sigiriya is its mirrored walls. In the old days it was so refined that the king could see the reflection. The mirror walls are painted with inscriptions and poems written for Sigiriya&#8217;s guests.</p><p>The oldest inscription is from the ninth century. The inscription says that Sigiriya was a tourist destination more than a thousand years ago. Today it is strictly forbidden to paint walls.</p>								</div>
				</div>
					</div>
		</div>
					</div>
		</section>

						<div class="elementor-container elementor-column-gap-default">
					<div class="elementor-column elementor-col-100 elementor-top-column elementor-element elementor-element-801dd4a" data-id="801dd4a" data-element_type="column">

						<div class="elementor-container elementor-column-gap-default">
					<div class="elementor-column elementor-col-50 elementor-top-column elementor-element elementor-element-db37de2" data-id="db37de2" data-element_type="column">
			<div class="elementor-widget-wrap elementor-element-populated">
						<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-60fda99 elementor-position-top elementor-invisible elementor-widget elementor-widget-image-box" data-id="60fda99" data-element_type="widget" data-settings="{&quot;_animation&quot;:&quot;zoomIn&quot;}" data-widget_type="image-box.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
					<div class="elementor-image-box-wrapper"><figure class="elementor-image-box-img"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="480" height="320" src="https://sigiriyafortress.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/sigiriya_mirror_wall.jpg" class="attachment-large size-large wp-image-1849" alt="sigiriya_mirror_wall" title="Home 15" srcset="https://sigiriyafortress.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/sigiriya_mirror_wall.jpg 480w, https://sigiriyafortress.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/sigiriya_mirror_wall-300x200.jpg 300w" sizes="(max-width: 480px) 100vw, 480px" /></figure></div>				</div>
				</div>
					</div>
		</div>
				<div class="elementor-column elementor-col-50 elementor-top-column elementor-element elementor-element-e380dcb" data-id="e380dcb" data-element_type="column">
			<div class="elementor-widget-wrap elementor-element-populated">
						<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-9aef713 elementor-position-top elementor-invisible elementor-widget elementor-widget-image-box" data-id="9aef713" data-element_type="widget" data-settings="{&quot;_animation&quot;:&quot;slideInRight&quot;,&quot;_animation_mobile&quot;:&quot;none&quot;}" data-widget_type="image-box.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
					<div class="elementor-image-box-wrapper"><figure class="elementor-image-box-img"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="50" height="50" src="https://sigiriyafortress.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/pngwing.com-1.png" class="attachment-full size-full wp-image-4741" alt="pngwing.com 1" title="Home 16"></figure><div class="elementor-image-box-content"><h3 class="elementor-image-box-title">1. Sigiriya MIrror wall</h3><p class="elementor-image-box-description">Just past the "Sigiriya Frescoes", you walk alongside what is known as the “Mirror Wall” — a wall polished so heavily that the king would have been able to see his reflection on the surface. You’ll see names and notes scribbled into the wall, some from as early as the 8th century, by visitors to Sigiriya Lions Rock.<br><br>

One translated writing reads: “I am Budal [the writer's name]. Came with hundreds of people to see Sigiriya. Since all the others wrote poems, I did not!” Some things never change.<br><br>

Further graffiti nowadays is strictly banned in order to protect these ancient writings.</p></div></div>				</div>
				</div>
					</div>
		</div>
					</div>
		</section>
				<section class="elementor-section elementor-top-section elementor-element elementor-element-4b0a14d elementor-section-boxed elementor-section-height-default elementor-section-height-default" data-id="4b0a14d" data-element_type="section">
						<div class="elementor-container elementor-column-gap-default">
					<div class="elementor-column elementor-col-50 elementor-top-column elementor-element elementor-element-a4c8e8a" data-id="a4c8e8a" data-element_type="column">
			<div class="elementor-widget-wrap elementor-element-populated">
						<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-5bf8fd9 elementor-position-top elementor-invisible elementor-widget elementor-widget-image-box" data-id="5bf8fd9" data-element_type="widget" data-settings="{&quot;_animation&quot;:&quot;zoomIn&quot;}" data-widget_type="image-box.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
					<div class="elementor-image-box-wrapper"><figure class="elementor-image-box-img"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="480" height="320" src="https://sigiriyafortress.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/Sigiriya-Lion-paw-e1604633623656.jpg" class="attachment-large size-large wp-image-1850" alt="Sigiriya lion rock" title="Home 17" srcset="https://sigiriyafortress.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/Sigiriya-Lion-paw-e1604633623656.jpg 480w, https://sigiriyafortress.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/Sigiriya-Lion-paw-e1604633623656-300x200.jpg 300w" sizes="(max-width: 480px) 100vw, 480px" /></figure></div>				</div>
				</div>
					</div>
		</div>
				<div class="elementor-column elementor-col-50 elementor-top-column elementor-element elementor-element-6c27b61" data-id="6c27b61" data-element_type="column">
			<div class="elementor-widget-wrap elementor-element-populated">
						<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-6ec8b3e elementor-position-top elementor-invisible elementor-widget elementor-widget-image-box" data-id="6ec8b3e" data-element_type="widget" data-settings="{&quot;_animation&quot;:&quot;slideInRight&quot;,&quot;_animation_mobile&quot;:&quot;none&quot;}" data-widget_type="image-box.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
					<div class="elementor-image-box-wrapper"><figure class="elementor-image-box-img"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="50" height="50" src="https://sigiriyafortress.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/pngwing.com-1.png" class="attachment-full size-full wp-image-4741" alt="pngwing.com 1" title="Home 16"></figure><div class="elementor-image-box-content"><h3 class="elementor-image-box-title">2. Sigiriya Lion's Paw</h3><p class="elementor-image-box-description">At the northern end of the Sigiriya Lion Rock, a narrow pathway emerges on to the large platform from which the site derives its name – Sigiriya (from sinha-giri) means 'Lions Rock'. HCP Bell, the British archaeologist responsible for an enormous amount of archaeology in Sri Lanka, found the two enormous lion paws when excavating in 1898.<br><br>

The final ascent to the top commenced with a stairway that led between the Sigiriya lion’s paws and into its mouth.
<br><br>
The 5th-century lion has since disappeared, apart from the first steps and the paws. Reaching the top means clambering up across a series of metal stairs, but you can still see the original grooves and steps cut into the Sigiriya Lion Rock.</p></div></div>				</div>
				</div>
					</div>
		</div>
					</div>
		</section>
				<section class="elementor-section elementor-top-section elementor-element elementor-element-abc7a53 elementor-section-boxed elementor-section-height-default elementor-section-height-default" data-id="abc7a53" data-element_type="section">
						<div class="elementor-container elementor-column-gap-default">
					<div class="elementor-column elementor-col-50 elementor-top-column elementor-element elementor-element-5231e63" data-id="5231e63" data-element_type="column">
			<div class="elementor-widget-wrap elementor-element-populated">
						<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-5dec8ab elementor-position-top elementor-invisible elementor-widget elementor-widget-image-box" data-id="5dec8ab" data-element_type="widget" data-settings="{&quot;_animation&quot;:&quot;zoomIn&quot;}" data-widget_type="image-box.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
					<div class="elementor-image-box-wrapper"><figure class="elementor-image-box-img"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="480" height="320" src="https://sigiriyafortress.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/SIGIRIYA-FRESCOES.jpg" class="attachment-large size-large wp-image-1851" alt="about sigiriya" title="Home 19" srcset="https://sigiriyafortress.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/SIGIRIYA-FRESCOES.jpg 480w, https://sigiriyafortress.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/SIGIRIYA-FRESCOES-300x200.jpg 300w" sizes="(max-width: 480px) 100vw, 480px" /></figure></div>				</div>
				</div>
					</div>
		</div>
				<div class="elementor-column elementor-col-50 elementor-top-column elementor-element elementor-element-e4cc4c1" data-id="e4cc4c1" data-element_type="column">
			<div class="elementor-widget-wrap elementor-element-populated">
						<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-2a32480 elementor-position-top elementor-invisible elementor-widget elementor-widget-image-box" data-id="2a32480" data-element_type="widget" data-settings="{&quot;_animation&quot;:&quot;slideInRight&quot;,&quot;_animation_mobile&quot;:&quot;none&quot;}" data-widget_type="image-box.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
					<div class="elementor-image-box-wrapper"><figure class="elementor-image-box-img"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="50" height="50" src="https://sigiriyafortress.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/pngwing.com-1.png" class="attachment-full size-full wp-image-4741" alt="pngwing.com 1" title="Home 16"></figure><div class="elementor-image-box-content"><h3 class="elementor-image-box-title">3. Sigiriya Frescoes</h3><p class="elementor-image-box-description">After passing the gardens, you’ll approach a staircase which slowly winds its way up Sigiriya Lion Rock. One section of the staircase will allow you to view some of the ancient frescoes painted on the Sigiriya cave walls. These paintings are similar to those of the Anuradhapura period but have a distinct style in the way the lines and shadows are drawn. <br><br>

To add to how impressive these ancient Sigiriya paintings are, it’s believe that the original paintings would have covered the entire face of Sigiriya Lions Rock — an area 140 meters long and 40 meters high.<br><br>

Definitely take the extra few minutes to view the paintings and try to imagine what Sigiriya Rock would have looked like in all its painted glory thousands of years ago. As John Still suggested in 1907: “The whole face of the hill appears to have been a gigantic picture gallery . . . the largest picture in the world perhaps”</p></div></div>				</div>
				</div>
					</div>
		</div>
					</div>
		</section>
				<section class="elementor-section elementor-top-section elementor-element elementor-element-db74e50 elementor-section-boxed elementor-section-height-default elementor-section-height-default" data-id="db74e50" data-element_type="section">
						<div class="elementor-container elementor-column-gap-default">
					<div class="elementor-column elementor-col-50 elementor-top-column elementor-element elementor-element-fa2ab84" data-id="fa2ab84" data-element_type="column">
			<div class="elementor-widget-wrap elementor-element-populated">
						<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-3947a72 elementor-position-top elementor-invisible elementor-widget elementor-widget-image-box" data-id="3947a72" data-element_type="widget" data-settings="{&quot;_animation&quot;:&quot;zoomIn&quot;}" data-widget_type="image-box.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
					<div class="elementor-image-box-wrapper"><figure class="elementor-image-box-img"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="480" height="321" src="https://sigiriyafortress.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/Lion-palace-sigiriya.jpg" class="attachment-large size-large wp-image-1852" alt="Things to do in Sigiriya" title="Home 21" srcset="https://sigiriyafortress.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/Lion-palace-sigiriya.jpg 480w, https://sigiriyafortress.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/Lion-palace-sigiriya-300x201.jpg 300w" sizes="(max-width: 480px) 100vw, 480px" /></figure></div>				</div>
				</div>
					</div>
		</div>
				<div class="elementor-column elementor-col-50 elementor-top-column elementor-element elementor-element-c25150a" data-id="c25150a" data-element_type="column">
			<div class="elementor-widget-wrap elementor-element-populated">
						<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-cdeecda elementor-position-top elementor-invisible elementor-widget elementor-widget-image-box" data-id="cdeecda" data-element_type="widget" data-settings="{&quot;_animation&quot;:&quot;slideInRight&quot;,&quot;_animation_mobile&quot;:&quot;none&quot;}" data-widget_type="image-box.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
					<div class="elementor-image-box-wrapper"><figure class="elementor-image-box-img"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="50" height="50" src="https://sigiriyafortress.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/pngwing.com-1.png" class="attachment-full size-full wp-image-4741" alt="pngwing.com 1" title="Home 16"></figure><div class="elementor-image-box-content"><h2 class="elementor-image-box-title">4. Sigiriya Boulder Gardens</h2><p class="elementor-image-box-description">As you enter Sigiriya Lions Rock, you’ll first walk through a series of beautiful gardens as you make your way to the towering Lion’s Rock ahead.<br><br>

The water gardens, cave and boulder gardens, and terraces gardens at Sigiriya are among the oldest landscaped gardens in the world, so be sure to take some time to appreciate them!</p></div></div>				</div>
				</div>
					</div>
		</div>
					</div>
		</section>

			<script>
				const lazyloadRunObserver = () => {
					const lazyloadBackgrounds = document.querySelectorAll( `.e-con.e-parent:not(.e-lazyloaded)` );
					const lazyloadBackgroundObserver = new IntersectionObserver( ( entries ) => {
						entries.forEach( ( entry ) => {
							if ( entry.isIntersecting ) {
								let lazyloadBackground = entry.target;
								if( lazyloadBackground ) {
									lazyloadBackground.classList.add( 'e-lazyloaded' );
								}
								lazyloadBackgroundObserver.unobserve( entry.target );
							}
						});
					}, { rootMargin: '200px 0px 200px 0px' } );
					lazyloadBackgrounds.forEach( ( lazyloadBackground ) => {
						lazyloadBackgroundObserver.observe( lazyloadBackground );
					} );
				};
				const events = [
					'DOMContentLoaded',
					'elementor/lazyload/observe',
				];
				events.forEach( ( event ) => {
					document.addEventListener( event, lazyloadRunObserver );
				} );
			</script>
